In May 2021, AT&amp;T <a data-ylk="elm:context_link;itc:0" href="https://about.att.com/story/2021/warnermedia_discovery.html" target="_blank">announced</a> that it was spinning off that division and merging it with Discovery in a $43 billion deal.
